001|# Product Requirement Document for Event Website SaaS Platform
002|
003|## 1. Language & Project Info
004|- **Language**: English
005|- **Programming Language**: Python (Django) or Node.js (Express)
006|- **Project Name**: event_website_saas
007|
008|## 2. Restated Requirements
009|Create a responsive web application for users to create personalized event websites with features including an editor, template selection, guest RSVP tracking, payment gateway integration, cloud image storage, and a basic admin panel, ensuring low hosting and storage costs.
010|
011|## 3. Product Definition
012|### Product Goals
013|1. Enable users to create personalized event websites easily and efficiently.
014|2. Provide a seamless RSVP tracking system for event organizers.
015|3. Ensure low hosting and storage costs for the platform.
016|
017|### User Stories
018|1. As an event organizer, I want to create a personalized event website so that I can promote my event effectively.
019|2. As a user, I want to select from various templates so that I can customize my event website according to my theme.
020|3. As an organizer, I want to track guest RSVPs so that I can manage my event attendance.
021|4. As a user, I want to make payments securely through a payment gateway so that I can confirm my attendance.
022|5. As an admin, I want to manage user accounts and events through a basic admin panel so that I can oversee the platform's operations.
023|
024|### Competitive Analysis
025|- **Product A**: Pros: User-friendly interface, multiple templates. Cons: High hosting costs.
026|- **Product B**: Pros: Good RSVP tracking. Cons: Limited customization options.
027|- **Product C**: Pros: Affordable pricing. Cons: Lacks payment gateway integration.
028|- **Product D**: Pros: Cloud storage included. Cons: Complicated admin panel.
029|- **Product E**: Pros: Responsive design. Cons: Limited features.
030|
031|### Competitive Quadrant Chart
032|```mermaid
033|quadrantChart
034|    title "Competitive Analysis of Event Website Platforms"
035|    x-axis "Low Cost" --> "High Cost"
036|    y-axis "Low Features" --> "High Features"
037|    quadrant-1 "Best Value"
038|    quadrant-2 "Needs Improvement"
039|    quadrant-3 "Underperforming"
040|    quadrant-4 "High-End"
041|    "Product A": [0.8, 0.9]
042|    "Product B": [0.6, 0.7]
043|    "Product C": [0.9, 0.5]
044|    "Product D": [0.4, 0.8]
045|    "Product E": [0.5, 0.6]
046|```
047|

049|### Requirements Analysis
050|- **Editor**: A user-friendly editor for creating event websites.
051|- **Template Selection**: A variety of templates for users to choose from.
052|- **RSVP Tracking**: A system to track guest responses.
053|- **Payment Gateway**: Integration with popular payment gateways.
054|- **Cloud Storage**: For storing images and event-related files.
055|- **Admin Panel**: Basic functionalities for managing users and events.
056|

001|# Product Requirement Document for Event Website SaaS Platform
002|
003|## 1. Language & Project Info
004|- **Language**: English
005|- **Programming Language**: Python (Django) or Node.js (Express)
006|- **Project Name**: event_website_saas
007|
008|## 2. Restated Requirements
009|Create a responsive web application for users to create personalized event websites with features including an editor, template selection, guest RSVP tracking, payment gateway integration, cloud image storage, and a basic admin panel, ensuring low hosting and storage costs.
010|
011|## 3. Product Definition
012|### Product Goals
013|1. Enable users to create personalized event websites easily and efficiently.
014|2. Provide a seamless RSVP tracking system for event organizers.
015|3. Ensure low hosting and storage costs for the platform.
016|
017|### User Stories
018|1. As an event organizer, I want to create a personalized event website so that I can promote my event effectively.
019|2. As a user, I want to select from various templates so that I can customize my event website according to my theme.
020|3. As an organizer, I want to track guest RSVPs so that I can manage my event attendance.
021|4. As a user, I want to make payments securely through a payment gateway so that I can confirm my attendance.
022|5. As an admin, I want to manage user accounts and events through a basic admin panel so that I can oversee the platform's operations.
023|
024|### Competitive Analysis
025|- **Product A**: Pros: User-friendly interface, multiple templates. Cons: High hosting costs.
026|- **Product B**: Pros: Good RSVP tracking. Cons: Limited customization options.
027|- **Product C**: Pros: Affordable pricing. Cons: Lacks payment gateway integration.
028|- **Product D**: Pros: Cloud storage included. Cons: Complicated admin panel.
029|- **Product E**: Pros: Responsive design. Cons: Limited features.
030|
031|### Competitive Quadrant Chart
032|```mermaid
033|quadrantChart
034|    title "Competitive Analysis of Event Website Platforms"
035|    x-axis "Low Cost" --> "High Cost"
036|    y-axis "Low Features" --> "High Features"

038|    quadrant-2 "Needs Improvement"
039|    quadrant-3 "Underperforming"
040|    quadrant-4 "High-End"
041|    "Product A": [0.8, 0.9]
042|    "Product B": [0.6, 0.7]
043|    "Product C": [0.9, 0.5]
044|    "Product D": [0.4, 0.8]
045|    "Product E": [0.5, 0.6]
046|```
047|
048|## 4. Technical Specifications
049|### Requirements Analysis
050|- **Editor**: A user-friendly editor for creating event websites.
051|- **Template Selection**: A variety of templates for users to choose from.
052|- **RSVP Tracking**: A system to track guest responses.
053|- **Payment Gateway**: Integration with popular payment gateways.
054|- **Cloud Storage**: For storing images and event-related files.
055|- **Admin Panel**: Basic functionalities for managing users and events.
056|
057|### Requirements Pool
058|- **P0**: Editor, Template Selection, RSVP Tracking
059|- **P1**: Payment Gateway Integration, Cloud Storage
060|- **P2**: Admin Panel
061|

068|- Are there any specific compliance requirements for data storage?
069|

074|
